# üîÄ BRANCHING-PATHS-KOMPLETT

## DECISION-TREE-MASTER

**MAJOR-DECISION-POINTS:** 8

### DECISION-01: Interview-mit-Journalist

**PUNKT:** T+290000ms

- Kooperativ: Media-Bonus +TV-Appearance +Reputation
- Ablehnen: Neutral
- Abweisend: Media-Penalty -Reputation

### DECISION-02: Deeskalation-vs-Festnahme

**PUNKT:** T+702000ms  
**OPTIONEN:** Direkt-Festnehmen / Deeskalation / Verst√§rkung-Abwarten  
**KONSEQUENZEN:**
- Deeskalation: Best-Outcome +Bonus-XP +Karma
- Direkt: Quick-aber-Gewaltrisiko
- Warten: Safe-aber-Mission-Risk

### DECISION-03: Vernehmung-Schuldfrage

**PUNKT:** T+960000ms  
**OPTIONEN:** Schuldig / Grauzone / Unschuldig  
**KONSEQUENZEN:**
- Influences-Weber-Decision
- Changes-Player-Karma
- Affects-Story-Later

### DECISION-04: Krause-Freilassen-oder-Festhalten

**PUNKT:** T+1025000ms

- Festhalten: Crowd-Riot +Phase-4-Combat
- Kompromiss: Mixed

### DECISION-05: Exit-Front-oder-Hinterausgang

- Hinten: Quick-End -Bonus-XP

## ENDINGS-VARIATIONEN

**ENDING-A: PERFEKT (5-Sterne)**

- Unlocks: Special-Skill

**ENDING-B: GUT (4-Sterne)**

- Rewards: Good-XP +Karma
- Unlocks: Standard-Progression

**ENDING-C: BEFRIEDIGEND (3-Sterne)**
- Bedingungen: Mission-Success + Moderate-Violence
- Rewards: Standard-XP
- Unlocks: Basic-Progression

**ENDING-D: AUSREICHEND (2-Sterne)**
- Bedingungen: Mission-Success + Heavy-Violence + Many-Injuries
- Rewards: Low-XP -Karma
- Unlocks: Progression-mit-Penalties

**ENDING-F: GESCHEITERT (1-Stern)**
- Bedingungen: Objectives-Failed oder-Mass-Casualties
- Consequences: Mission-Restart oder-Story-Alt-Path
- Penalties: No-Progression

# üéÆ GAMEPLAY-MECHANICS-DETAILED

## DEESKALATION-SYSTEM-MECHANICS

**SYSTEM-OVERVIEW:**
- Deeskalation-ist-Skill-Baum-F√§higkeit
- Leveled-Up durch-Verwendung
- Multiple-Techniken-verf√ºgbar

**LEVEL-1-TECHNIKEN:**
- Ruhige-Stimme: Reduziert-NPC-Aggression-5-Prozent
- Offene-K√∂rpersprache: NPCs-Less-Defensive
- Aktives-Zuh√∂ren: NPCs-Feel-Heard

**LEVEL-2-TECHNIKEN:**
- Empathie-Zeigen: Reduziert-Aggression-10-Prozent
- Kompromiss-Anbieten: NPCs-Accept-Partial-Solutions
- Humor-Einsetzen: Entspannt-Situation

**LEVEL-3-TECHNIKEN:**
- Meisterhafte-Verhandlung: 20-Prozent-Aggression-Reduktion
- Crowd-Splitting: Divide-Group-Into-Smaller-Parts
- Autorit√§ts-Balance: Firm-But-Fair-Respected

**SKILL-TREE-PROGRESSION:**
- XP-Required-Level-2: 500-XP
- XP-Required-Level-3: 1500-XP
- XP-Required-Master: 3000-XP

**SUCCESS-CALCULATION:**
```
Success-Chance = (Base-Chance + Skill-Level * 10 + Charisma * 5 + Situation-Modifier) %

Base-Chance: 30%
Skill-Level: 0-3
Charisma: Player-Stat 1-10
Situation-Modifier: -20 to +20 (context-dependent)

Example: Level-2-Skill + 7-Charisma + Neutral-Situation
= 30 + (2*10) + (7*5) + 0 = 30 + 20 + 35 = 85% Success
```

# üéµ AUDIO-MIX-SPECIFICATIONS-COMPLETE

## MASTER-MIX-TARGETS

**OVERALL-DYNAMIC-RANGE:** -60dB to 0dB  
**PEAK-LIMITER:** -0.3dB ceiling  
**RMS-AVERAGE:** -18dB target  
**FREQUENCY-RESPONSE:** 20Hz-20kHz  

## CATEGORY-LEVELS

### DIALOGUE-MIX

**PRIORITY:** Highest always-Clear  
**FREQUENCY:** 300Hz-8kHz emphasis  
**COMPRESSION:** 3:1-ratio threshold--20dB  
**EQ-STANDARD:**
- High-Pass-Filter: 80Hz-Remove-Rumble
- Presence-Boost: +3dB at 2-3kHz
- De-Ess: -6dB at 6-8kHz reduce-Sibilance
- Low-Pass-Filter: 12kHz natural

**CHARACTER-SPECIFIC:**

**WEBER-VOICE:**
- Base-Level: -10dB
- EQ: +2dB at 150Hz chest-Resonance
- Reverb: Room-Ambience 0.3s-Decay
- Compression: Heavy 4:1 authority

**KRAUSE-VOICE:**
- Base-Level: -5dB (louder-Passionate)
- EQ: +4dB at 200-400Hz power
- Megaphone-Effect: Bandpass-400Hz-3kHz distortion-10-percent
- Compression: 2:1 dynamic-Preserving
- Reverb: Outdoor-Space 0.8s-Decay

**KOVACS-VOICE:**
- Base-Level: -8dB
- EQ: +3dB at 1-2kHz clarity
- Reverb: Subtle-Room 0.2s
- Compression: 3:1 balanced

**CROWD-VOICES:**
- Base-Level: -15dB (background)
- EQ: Midrange-Emphasis-1kHz
- Reverb: Large-Space 1.5s-Decay
- Compression: 2:1 allow-Dynamics

### MUSIC-MIX

**PRIORITY:** Low submissive-to-Dialogue  
**DYNAMIC-AUTOMATION:** Ducking when-Dialogue-active  
**DUCK-AMOUNT:** -8dB during-Speech  
**DUCK-TIME:** Attack-100ms Release-500ms  

**CUTSCENE-MUSIC:**
- Base-Level: -25dB
- Peak-Level: -15dB (during-Action)
- EQ: Slight-High-Cut-8kHz warm
- Compression: 2:1 gentle
- Stereo-Width: Full-100-percent

**GAMEPLAY-MUSIC:**
- Base-Level: -30dB
- Dynamic-Scaling: With-Tension-Meter
  - Low-Tension: -30dB
  - Medium-Tension: -25dB
  - High-Tension: -20dB
- EQ: Clear-Midrange vocals-If-Present
- Compression: 2:1 transparent

### SFX-MIX

**PRIORITY:** Medium varies-By-Importance  

**CRITICAL-SFX (Player-Actions):**
- Footsteps: -15dB
- Weapon-Sounds: -8dB
- UI-Clicks: -18dB
- Pain-Sounds: -10dB

- Siren: -8dB

- Algorithm: HRTF binaural
- Distance-Attenuation: Inverse-Square-Law
- Doppler-Effect: Speed-Of-Sound 343m-s
- Occlusion: Ray-Trace-Based attenuation-By-Geometry

  - Body-Mesh: 85.000-Triangles (High-Detail-Musculature Anatomically-Accurate Visible-Veins-Tendons)
  - Hair-System: 35.000-Triangles (Real-Polygon-Hair-Strands not-Hair-Cards with-Physics-Simulation)

## SHADER-SYSTEM-DETAILS

### PBR-MATERIAL-SHADER

**VERTEX-SHADER-OPERATIONS:**
- Position-Transform: Model-View-Projection-Matrix
- Normal-Transform: Normal-Matrix-for-Lighting
- Tangent-Transform: For-Normal-Mapping
- UV-Coordinates: Pass-Through-to-Fragment
- Shadow-Coordinates: Light-Space-Transform

**FRAGMENT-SHADER-OPERATIONS:**

**TEXTURE-SAMPLING:**
- Albedo-Map: Base-Color RGB
- Normal-Map: Tangent-Space-Normals
- Metalness-Map: Grayscale-Value
- Roughness-Map: Grayscale-Value
- AO-Map: Ambient-Occlusion-Grayscale

**LIGHTING-CALCULATION:**
```
For each Light:
  Calculate Light-Direction
  Calculate View-Direction
  Calculate Half-Vector (Light + View)
  
  NdotL = dot(Normal, Light-Direction)
  NdotV = dot(Normal, View-Direction)
  NdotH = dot(Normal, Half-Vector)
  
  Diffuse = NdotL * Albedo * (1 - Metalness)
  
  Fresnel = F0 + (1 - F0) * pow(1 - NdotV, 5)
  where F0 = lerp(0.04, Albedo, Metalness)
  
  D (Distribution) = GGX-Function(NdotH, Roughness)
  G (Geometry) = Smith-GGX(NdotV, NdotL, Roughness)
  
  Specular = (D * G * Fresnel) / (4 * NdotV * NdotL)
  
  Final-Color = Diffuse + Specular
  Final-Color *= Shadow-Value
  Final-Color *= AO-Value
  Final-Color += Emission (if-any)
```

**GGX-FUNCTIONS:**
```
GGX-Distribution:
  alpha = Roughness^2
  alpha2 = alpha^2
  denom = NdotH^2 * (alpha2 - 1) + 1
  D = alpha2 / (PI * denom^2)

Smith-GGX-Geometry:
  k = (Roughness + 1)^2 / 8
  G1(v) = v / (v * (1 - k) + k)
  G = G1(NdotV) * G1(NdotL)
```

### POST-PROCESSING-SHADERS

**BLOOM-SHADER:**

**PASS-1-BRIGHT-EXTRACT:**
```
For each Pixel:
  Color = Sample-Scene-Texture
  Luminance = dot(Color.rgb, vec3(0.2126, 0.7152, 0.0722))
  
  if Luminance > Threshold (1.0):
    Bright-Color = Color * (Luminance - Threshold)
  else:
    Bright-Color = vec3(0)
  
  Output = Bright-Color
```

**PASS-2-BLUR-HORIZONTAL:**
```
Gaussian-Blur 9-Tap:
  Weights = [0.05, 0.09, 0.12, 0.15, 0.16, 0.15, 0.12, 0.09, 0.05]
  
  For each Pixel:
    Sum = 0
    For i = -4 to 4:
      Sample = Sample-Texture(UV + vec2(i * TexelSize.x, 0))
      Sum += Sample * Weights[i + 4]
    
    Output = Sum
```

**PASS-3-BLUR-VERTICAL:**
```
Same-As-Horizontal but:
  Offset = vec2(0, i * TexelSize.y)
```

**PASS-4-COMPOSITE:**
```
For each Pixel:
  Scene-Color = Sample-Scene-Texture
  Bloom-Color = Sample-Bloom-Texture
  
  Final-Color = Scene-Color + Bloom-Color * Intensity (0.5)
  Output = Final-Color
```

**SSAO-SHADER (Screen-Space-Ambient-Occlusion):**

**PASS-1-SSAO-CALCULATION:**
```
For each Pixel:
  Position = Reconstruct-From-Depth
  Normal = Sample-Normal-Texture
  Random-Vector = Sample-Noise-Texture (4x4-Tiling)
  
  Occlusion = 0
  For i = 0 to Sample-Count (16):
    Sample-Position = Generate-Sample-In-Hemisphere(Normal, Random-Vector)
    Offset = Position + Sample-Position * Radius (0.5)
    
    Projected = Project-To-Screen-Space(Offset)
    Sample-Depth = Sample-Depth-Texture(Projected)
    
    Range-Check = smoothstep(0, 1, Radius / abs(Position.z - Sample-Depth))
    
    if Sample-Depth < Offset.z:
      Occlusion += Range-Check
  
  Occlusion /= Sample-Count
  Output = 1.0 - Occlusion
```

**PASS-2-SSAO-BLUR:**
```
Bilateral-Blur:
  For each Pixel:
    Sum = 0
    Weight-Sum = 0
    
    For offset in Kernel (4x4):
      Sample = Sample-SSAO-Texture(UV + offset)
      Depth-Diff = abs(Center-Depth - Sample-Depth)
      Weight = exp(-Depth-Diff * 10)
      
      Sum += Sample * Weight
      Weight-Sum += Weight
    
    Output = Sum / Weight-Sum
```

## PHYSICS-ENGINE-INTEGRATION-DETAILS

### CHARACTER-CONTROLLER-SPECIFICATIONS

**CAPSULE-COLLIDER:**
- Height: 1.8-Meter (Character-Height)
- Radius: 0.3-Meter (Character-Width-Half)
- Center-Offset: (0, 0.9, 0) Capsule-Center-at-Waist
- Material: Friction-0.0 (no-Sliding-Resistance)
- Restitution: 0.0 (no-Bouncing)

**MOVEMENT-PHYSICS:**

**GROUND-MOVEMENT:**
```
Input-Vector = Normalize(WASD-Input)
Target-Velocity = Input-Vector * Move-Speed (2.0 m/s)

Current-Velocity = Get-Current-Velocity()
Velocity-Change = Target-Velocity - Current-Velocity

Acceleration = 10.0 m/s^2
Max-Velocity-Change = Acceleration * Delta-Time

Clamped-Change = Clamp(Velocity-Change, -Max-Velocity-Change, Max-Velocity-Change)

Apply-Force(Clamped-Change * Mass)
```

**JUMP-PHYSICS:**
```
if Is-Grounded and Jump-Button-Pressed:
  Jump-Force = sqrt(2 * Gravity * Jump-Height)
  where Jump-Height = 1.2 meters
        Gravity = 9.8 m/s^2
  
  Jump-Force = sqrt(2 * 9.8 * 1.2) = 4.85 m/s
  
  Apply-Impulse(0, Jump-Force * Mass, 0)
```

**GROUND-DETECTION:**
```
Raycast-Parameters:
  Origin = Character-Bottom-Center (0, 0.1, 0)
  Direction = Down (0, -1, 0)
  Max-Distance = 0.15-Meter
  Layer-Mask = Ground-Layer
  
if Raycast-Hits:
  Is-Grounded = true
  Ground-Normal = Hit.Normal
else:
  Is-Grounded = false
```

**SLOPE-HANDLING:**
```
Max-Slope-Angle = 45-Degrees

Ground-Angle = Angle-Between(Ground-Normal, Vector-Up)

if Ground-Angle > Max-Slope-Angle:
  Slide-Down-Slope
  Slide-Direction = Project-On-Plane(Gravity, Ground-Normal)
  Apply-Force(Slide-Direction * 5.0)
```

### CROWD-PHYSICS-SYSTEM

**COLLISION-AVOIDANCE:**

**LOCAL-AVOIDANCE-ALGORITHM (Reciprocal-Velocity-Obstacles):**

```
For each NPC:
  Preferred-Velocity = Path-Direction * Desired-Speed
  
  For each Nearby-NPC (within 5m):
    Relative-Position = Other.Position - This.Position
    Relative-Velocity = Other.Velocity - This.Velocity
    
    Time-To-Collision = Compute-TTC(Relative-Position, Relative-Velocity, Combined-Radius)
    
    if Time-To-Collision < 3-Seconds:
      Avoidance-Vector = Compute-Avoidance(Relative-Position, Relative-Velocity)
      Preferred-Velocity += Avoidance-Vector
  
  Final-Velocity = Lerp(Current-Velocity, Preferred-Velocity, 0.5)
  Apply-Velocity(Final-Velocity)
```

**CROWD-DENSITY-MANAGEMENT:**

```
Grid-Cell-Size = 2-Meter-Squares

For each Cell:
  NPCs-In-Cell = Count-NPCs-In-Cell()
  Density = NPCs-In-Cell / Cell-Area
  
  if Density > Max-Density (4 NPCs/m^2):
    For each NPC in Cell:
      Push-Away-From-Center
      Reduce-Speed by 50-Percent
```

**PUSHING-AND-SHOVING:**

```
if NPC-Touches-Other-NPC:
  Contact-Normal = Normalize(This.Position - Other.Position)
  
  if Is-Aggressive:
    Push-Force = 200-Newtons
  else:
    Push-Force = 50-Newtons
  
  Apply-Impulse-To-Other(Contact-Normal * Push-Force)
  
  if Other-Is-Player:
    Camera-Shake(0.1-Intensity, 0.2-Duration)
```

## MEMORY-MANAGEMENT-STRATEGIES

### OBJECT-POOLING-SYSTEM

**POOLABLE-OBJECTS:**
- NPCs: Pool-Size-200
- Audio-Sources: Pool-Size-100
- Particle-Systems: Pool-Size-50
- UI-Elements: Pool-Size-30

**POOL-IMPLEMENTATION:**

```
Class-Object-Pool<T>:
  List<T> Available-Objects
  List<T> Active-Objects
  
  Function Get-Object():
    if Available-Objects.Count > 0:
      Object = Available-Objects.Pop()
    else:
      Object = Create-New-Object()
    
    Active-Objects.Add(Object)
    Object.On-Spawn()
    return Object
  
  Function Return-Object(Object):
    Object.On-Despawn()
    Active-Objects.Remove(Object)
    Available-Objects.Add(Object)
```

**BENEFITS:**
- Reduce-GC-Pressure: No-Constant-Allocation-Deallocation
- Faster-Spawning: Objects-Pre-Initialized
- Predictable-Performance: No-Allocation-Spikes

### ASSET-STREAMING-SYSTEM

**TEXTURE-STREAMING:**

```
For each Texture:
  Distance-To-Camera = Calculate-Distance()
  
  Required-Mip-Level = Calculate-Mip-Level(Distance-To-Camera, Screen-Size)
  Current-Mip-Level = Get-Loaded-Mip-Level()
  
  if Required-Mip-Level < Current-Mip-Level:
    Load-Higher-Resolution-Mip-Async()
  
  if Required-Mip-Level > Current-Mip-Level + 1:
    Unload-Lower-Resolution-Mip()
```

**MESH-STREAMING:**

```
For each Mesh:
  if Is-Visible and Distance < LOD-0-Distance:
    if Not-Loaded-LOD-0:
      Load-LOD-0-Async()
  
  if Not-Visible-For-Duration > 30-Seconds:
    Unload-All-LODs()
```

### GARBAGE-COLLECTION-OPTIMIZATION

**MANUAL-GC-SCHEDULING:**

```
During-Gameplay:
  Disable-Automatic-GC = true
  
During-Safe-Moments (Loading-Screens, Pauses):
  if Time-Since-Last-GC > 60-Seconds:
    System.GC.Collect()
    System.GC.WaitForPendingFinalizers()
```

**REDUCE-ALLOCATIONS:**
- Use-StringBuilder instead-of-String-Concatenation
- Cache-Component-References no-GetComponent-Per-Frame
- Reuse-Arrays and-Lists clear-Instead-Of-New
- Use-Struct-for-Small-Data-Types

**WEIGHT-RANGES:**
- Minimum-Value: 0.0 (neutral-No-Effect)
- Maximum-Value: 1.0 (full-Activation)
- Over-Activation-Possible: 1.2 (for-Exaggerated-Cartoon-Effects optional)
- Precision: 0.001 (three-Decimal-Places)

**BLENDING-METHOD:**
- Linear-Interpolation: NewVertex = BaseVertex + (TargetVertex minus BaseVertex) √ó Weight
- Multiple-Blendshapes: Additive-Blending allows-Combination
- Normalization: If-Total-Weight exceeds-1.0 normalize-Down

**MEMORY-LAYOUT:**
- Per-Blendshape: 45.000-Vertices √ó 3-Floats (X Y Z) = 540-KB
- 95-Blendshapes-Total: 95 √ó 540-KB = 51.3-MB per-Character
- Compression-Possible: Delta-Encoding reduces-to-15-MB

## CMP-PHASE-2: LIPSYNC-PHONEME-SYSTEM

### PHONEME-TO-VISEME-MAPPING

**DEUTSCHE-PHONEME (42-Sounds):**

**VOKALE (16-Phoneme):**
- [a] as-in "Vater": viseme_AA (mouth-Wide-Open)
- [aÀê] long-A: viseme_AA (sustained)
- […õ] as-in "Bett": viseme_E (mouth-Medium-Open)
- [e] as-in "Weg": viseme_E
- [i] as-in "mit": viseme_I (lips-Spread teeth-Close)
- [iÀê] long-I: viseme_I
- […î] as-in "Gott": viseme_O (lips-Round mouth-Open)
- [o] as-in "Boot": viseme_O
- [ ä] as-in "Mutter": viseme_U (lips-Round tight)
- [u] as-in "gut": viseme_U
- [y] as-in "√ºber": viseme_OE (German-Specific)
- [yÀê] long-√ú: viseme_OE
- [√∏] as-in "sch√∂n": viseme_OE
- [≈ì] as-in "√∂ffnen": viseme_OE
- […ô] schwa "bitte": viseme_ER (neutral-Relaxed)
- […ê] as-in "besser": viseme_ER

**KONSONANTEN (26-Phoneme):**

**BILABIAL (Lips-Together):**
- [p] [b] [m]: viseme_P (lips-Press-Together)
- Example: "Papa" "Baby" "Mama"

**LABIODENTAL (Lip-to-Teeth):**
- [f] [v]: viseme_F (upper-Teeth-Touch-Lower-Lip)
- Example: "Vater" "Wolf"

**DENTAL (Tongue-to-Teeth):**
- [t] [d] [n]: viseme_T (tongue-Tip-Behind-Upper-Teeth)
- Example: "Tag" "du" "Name"

**ALVEOLAR (Tongue-to-Gum):**
- [s] [z] [l] [r]: viseme_S (tongue-Near-Gum-Ridge)
- Example: "Sonne" "sein" "Licht" "Rot"

**POSTALVEOLAR (Tongue-Behind-Gum):**
- [ É] [ í] [t É] [d í]: viseme_SH (lips-Protrude tongue-Back)
- Example: "Schule" "Journal" "Deutsch"

**VELAR (Tongue-to-Soft-Palate):**
- [k] [g] [≈ã]: viseme_K (mouth-Slightly-Open tongue-Invisible)
- Example: "Kind" "Gott" "lang"

**GLOTTAL:**
- [h] [ î]: viseme_H (exhale-Visible-Breath)
- Example: "Haus" "be'erben" (Glottal-Stop)

**VISEME-TRANSITION-TIMING:**

**CO-ARTICULATION-RULES:**
When-Phonemes-Follow-Each-Other the-Mouth-Shape-Blends:

- Anticipatory-Co-Articulation: Mouth-Prepares-for-Next-Sound-Early
- Example: In-Word "Boot" the-[b]-Already-Shows-Lip-Rounding-for-[o]
- Timing: 50ms-Before-Sound-Starts

- Carryover-Co-Articulation: Previous-Sound-Affects-Current
- Example: After-[u]-Sound lips-Remain-Rounded-for-50ms

**BLENDING-WEIGHTS:**
- Current-Phoneme: 100-Percent-Weight at-Peak (middle-Of-Sound)
- Previous-Phoneme: Fades-Out-Over-50ms
- Next-Phoneme: Fades-In-Starting-50ms-Before

**SILENCE-HANDLING:**
- Between-Words: Return-to-Neutral (viseme_IDLE)
- Idle-Mouth: Lips-Slightly-Closed relaxed-Jaw
- Breathing: Subtle-Mouth-Opening-Every-3-Seconds

## CMP-PHASE-3: EYE-SYSTEM-ULTRA-DETAIL

### EYE-ANATOMY-MODELING

**SCLERA (White-Part):**
- Polygon-Count: 2.000-Triangles per-Eye
- Shape: Sphere-Segment radius-12mm
- Texture-Resolution: 2048x2048 (high-Detail-Veins)
- Shader-Properties:
  - Base-Color: RGB(245 245 245) slightly-Off-White
  - Roughness: 0.3 (semi-Glossy)
  - Subsurface-Scattering: Minimal (0.1)
  - Vein-Overlay: Red-Veins normal-Map alpha-Mask

**CORNEA (Transparent-Layer):**
- Polygon-Count: 500-Triangles per-Eye (high-Subdivision)
- Shape: Sphere-Bulge over-Iris radius-7.5mm
- Thickness: 0.5mm at-Center 1mm-at-Edge
- Shader-Properties:
  - Transparency: 0.95 (almost-Fully-Clear)
  - Refraction-IOR: 1.376 (realistic-Eye-Fluid)
  - Roughness: 0.05 (very-Smooth)
  - Fresnel-Effect: Strong (more-Reflection-at-Grazing-Angles)
  - Caustics: Enable (light-Focus-Through-Cornea)

**IRIS (Colored-Part):**
- Polygon-Count: 1.000-Triangles per-Eye (flat-Disk)
- Shape: Circle diameter-11mm
- Texture-Resolution: 4096x4096 (extreme-Detail-for-Close-Ups)
- Shader-Properties:
  - Base-Color: Custom-per-Character (Blue-Green-Brown-Gray-Hazel)
  - Detail-Layers:
    - Layer-1-Crypts: Dark-Lines-Radiating-from-Pupil
    - Layer-2-Collarette: Ring-Around-Pupil (lighter)
    - Layer-3-Furrows: Radial-Grooves
    - Layer-4-Limbal-Ring: Dark-Edge-Around-Iris
  - Normal-Map: 3D-Texture-Depth
  - Parallax-Mapping: Iris-Sits-Behind-Cornea (0.5mm-Depth)

**PUPIL (Black-Center):**
- Polygon-Count: Procedural (no-Geometry just-Shader)
- Shape: Perfect-Circle animated-Radius
- Dilation-Range:
  - Minimum: 1.5mm (bright-Light)
  - Maximum: 8mm (dark-Environment)
  - Speed: 0.5-Seconds-to-Adjust
- Dilation-Triggers:
  - Lighting: Auto-Adjust-to-Scene-Brightness
  - Emotion: Fear-Dilates Anger-Constricts (subtle)
  - Focus: Dilates-When-Looking-at-Close-Objects

**LENS (Internal-Not-Visible):**
- No-Geometry (handled-by-Cornea-Refraction)
- Affects: Light-Rays-Bending-Through-Eye

**TEAR-DUCT (Medial-Corner):**
- Polygon-Count: 300-Triangles
- Texture: Pink-Flesh-Color
- Wetness: Slightly-Shinier-Than-Surrounding-Skin
- Animation: Blink-Triggers-Subtle-Tear-Production

**TEAR-LINE (Water-Edge):**
- Polygon-Count: 200-Triangles (thin-Line-Along-Lower-Lid)
- Shader: Highly-Reflective (mirror-Like)
- Animation: Wobbles-Slightly-with-Eye-Movement
- Overflow: Can-Form-Tear-Drop if-Emotional-State-High

### EYE-MOVEMENT-SYSTEM

**SACCADES (Quick-Jumps):**
- Frequency: 3-4-Times-per-Second during-Normal-Activity
- Duration: 20-200ms depending-on-Distance
- Speed: Up-to-900-Degrees-per-Second
- Trajectory: Ballistic (cannot-Stop-Mid-Saccade)
- Overshoot: Slight-Overshoot-Then-Correct (realistic-Biology)

**SMOOTH-PURSUIT (Following-Moving-Object):**
- Speed: Up-to-30-Degrees-per-Second
- Lag: 100ms-Behind-Target (realistic-Neural-Delay)
- Catch-Up-Saccades: If-Target-Moves-Too-Fast

**MICROSACCADES (Tiny-Jitter):**
- Frequency: 1-2-Times-per-Second even-When-"Still"
- Amplitude: 0.1-0.5-Degrees (barely-Visible)
- Purpose: Prevents-Image-Fading (biological-Reason)
- Implementation: Random-Small-Movement every-0.5-Seconds

**VERGENCE (Eye-Convergence-for-Depth):**
- Near-Focus: Eyes-Converge (cross-Slightly)
- Far-Focus: Eyes-Parallel
- Transition-Speed: 0.3-Seconds
- Example: Looking-from-Far-Mountain to-Close-Hand

**VESTIBULO-OCULAR-REFLEX (Head-Movement-Compensation):**
- When-Head-Rotates: Eyes-Counter-Rotate to-Maintain-Gaze
- Gain: 1-to-1 (perfect-Compensation)
- Latency: 10ms (very-Fast)
- Example: Head-Turns-Right Eyes-Rotate-Left

### BLINK-ANIMATION-DETAILED

**BLINK-PHASES:**

**PHASE-1-CLOSING (80ms):**
- Frame-0-to-4 (at-60fps = 66ms):
  - Upper-Lid-Descends: 0-Percent to-100-Percent
  - Lower-Lid-Rises: 0-Percent to-20-Percent
  - Eyeball-Rolls-Up-Slightly: 5-Degrees (realistic-Biology)
  - Squash-Effect: Eyelid-Compresses-Vertically

**PHASE-2-CLOSED (20ms):**
- Frame-5 (33ms):
  - Upper-Lid: 100-Percent-Closed
  - Lower-Lid: 20-Percent
  - Hold-Position

**PHASE-3-OPENING (80ms):**
- Frame-6-to-9 (66ms):
  - Upper-Lid-Ascends: 100-Percent to-0-Percent
  - Lower-Lid-Descends: 20-Percent to-0-Percent
  - Eyeball-Rolls-Down: Back-to-Original-Position
  - Stretch-Effect: Eyelid-Extends-Vertically

**BLINK-FREQUENCY:**
- Normal: 15-20-Blinks-per-Minute (every-3-4-Seconds)
- Stressed: 25-30-Blinks-per-Minute
- Concentrated: 5-10-Blinks-per-Minute (suppressed)

**BLINK-VARIATIONS:**
- Half-Blink: 50-Percent-Closure (doubt-Expression)
- Slow-Blink: 300ms-Duration (tired or-Seductive)
- Flutter: Rapid-Sequence 5-Blinks (flirting or-Confusion)
- Wink: One-Eye-Only (intentional-Signal)

### EYE-GAZE-SYSTEM

**LOOK-AT-TARGET:**
- Input: 3D-World-Position (X Y Z)
- Calculate: Vector-from-Eye-to-Target
- Rotate: Eyeball-to-Align-with-Vector
- Constraints:
  - Max-Angle-from-Forward: 40-Degrees (before-Head-Turns)
  - Max-Up-Angle: 30-Degrees
  - Max-Down-Angle: 40-Degrees

**GAZE-BEHAVIORS:**

**CONVERSATION:**
- Look-at-Speaker's-Eyes: 70-Percent-of-Time
- Look-Away-Briefly: 30-Percent (thinking or-Listening)
- Direction-of-Look-Away: Up-Left (recalling) Down-Right (processing)

**IDLE:**
- Scan-Environment: Random-Points-of-Interest
- Dwell-Time: 1-3-Seconds per-Object
- Return-to-Neutral: Forward-Looking between-Scans

**COMBAT:**
- Lock-on-Target: Enemy-Center-of-Mass
- Quick-Glances: Check-Peripheral-Threats
- Anticipation: Look-Ahead-of-Moving-Targets

## CMP-PHASE-4: HAIR-SYSTEM-PRODUCTION

### HAIR-STRAND-GENERATION

**STRAND-BASED-HAIR (35.000-Polygons LOD-0):**

**STRAND-COUNT:**
- Total-Strands: 5.000-Visible-Strands (each-Strand-Represents-Cluster-of-Real-Hairs)
- Real-Hair-Count: ~100.000-Individual-Hairs (not-Rendered just-Represented)
- Poly-per-Strand: 7-Segments-per-Strand = 7-Polygons √ó 5.000 = 35.000-Total

**STRAND-ANATOMY:**
- Root: Attached-to-Scalp (fixed-Position)
- Mid-Sections: 5-Flexible-Segments
- Tip: Free-Floating (most-Movement)
- Width: 0.5mm-at-Root tapering-to-0.1mm-at-Tip

**STRAND-PLACEMENT-ALGORITHM:**

**STEP-1-SCALP-SURFACE:**
- Define-Scalp-Region: Face-Mesh-has-"Hair-Growth"-Vertex-Group
- Vertices-in-Group: ~2.000-Vertices on-Top-and-Back-of-Head
- Each-Vertex: Potential-Strand-Origin

**STEP-2-STRAND-DISTRIBUTION:**
- Density-Map: Texture (white = full-Density black = no-Hair)
- Variation: Procedural-Noise adds-Randomness
- Thinning-Areas: Temples-Slight-Receding (realistic for-Adult-Males)

**STEP-3-STRAND-DIRECTION:**
- Hair-Flow-Map: Vector-Field-Texture defines-Growth-Direction
- Typical-Patterns:
  - Top-of-Head: Flows-Backward-and-Outward-from-Crown
  - Sides: Flows-Downward-and-Back
  - Back: Straight-Down or-Slight-Forward-Curve
- Variation: Plus-Minus-20-Degrees-Random-per-Strand

**STEP-4-STRAND-LENGTH:**
- Base-Length: 15cm (for-Short-Hairstyle) up-to-60cm (for-Long-Hair)
- Variation: Gaussian-Distribution plus-minus-3cm
- Trimming: Some-Strands-Shorter (haircut-Imperfection)

**STEP-5-STRAND-CURLINESS:**
- Straight-Hair: Curliness-Factor-0.0
- Wavy-Hair: Curliness-0.3 (sine-Wave-along-Length)
- Curly-Hair: Curliness-0.7
- Kinky-Hair: Curliness-1.0 (tight-Coils)
- Formula: Position += Normal √ó sin(Length √ó Frequency √ó Curliness) √ó Amplitude

**STEP-6-CLUMPING:**
- Individual-Strands: Looks-Messy (too-Separated)
- Clumping-Algorithm: Group-5-10-Strands into-Cluster
- Method: Attract-Neighboring-Strands-Toward-Cluster-Center
- Strength: 0.5 (half-Way-Between-Individual-and-Merged)
- Result: Natural-Hair-Locks

**STEP-7-TAPERING:**
- Width-at-Root: 0.5mm
- Width-at-Mid: 0.3mm
- Width-at-Tip: 0.1mm (very-Fine)
- Mesh-Geometry: Cylinder-with-Variable-Radius

### HAIR-PHYSICS-SIMULATION

**POSITION-BASED-DYNAMICS (PBD):**

**CONSTRAINTS:**

**DISTANCE-CONSTRAINT (Maintain-Length):**
- Purpose: Each-Segment-Stays-Same-Length
- Formula: If-Distance-Between-Points-Not-Equal-Rest-Length then-Move-Points-Closer-or-Farther
- Iterations: 5-Solver-Iterations per-Frame
- Stiffness: 0.9 (almost-Rigid but-Slightly-Flexible)

**BENDING-CONSTRAINT (Prevent-Sharp-Angles):**
- Purpose: Hair-Doesn't-Fold-Unnaturally
- Formula: If-Angle-Between-Segments-Too-Sharp then-Rotate-to-Smoother-Angle
- Target-Angle: 180-Degrees (straight)
- Stiffness: 0.3 (allows-Some-Bending)

**COLLISION-CONSTRAINT (Hair-vs-Body):**
- Collision-Primitives: 20-Capsules-Approximating-Head-Neck-Shoulders
- Detection: Check-if-Hair-Strand-Intersects-Capsule
- Response: Push-Hair-Point-Outside-Capsule
- Friction: 0.5 (hair-Slides-Slightly on-Skin)

**SELF-COLLISION (Hair-vs-Hair):**
- Enabled: Only-for-LOD-0 (very-Expensive)
- Method: Spatial-Grid-Hashing (divide-Space-into-Cells)
- Check: Only-Strands-in-Same-or-Adjacent-Cells
- Response: Repulsion-Force (push-Away)
- Cost: 2ms-per-Frame (acceptable for-Close-View)

**EXTERNAL-FORCES:**

**GRAVITY:**
- Force: 9.81-m-per-s-squared downward
- Application: Each-Hair-Segment affected
- Result: Hair-Hangs-Down-Naturally

**WIND:**
- Input: Global-Wind-Vector (direction and-Speed)
- Turbulence: Perlin-Noise-adds-Variation
- Application: Force-Applied-to-All-Segments
- Damping: Hair-Doesn't-Instantly-Follow-Wind (lag-Effect)

**HEAD-MOVEMENT:**
- Inertia: When-Head-Moves hair-Lags-Behind
- Formula: Force = (Head-Velocity minus Hair-Velocity) √ó Damping
- Result: Hair-Swings-and-Bounces-with-Movement

**CONSTRAINTS-APPLICATION-ORDER:**

**FRAME-N:**
1. Apply-External-Forces (Gravity Wind Inertia)
2. Predict-New-Positions (Euler-Integration)
3. Solve-Distance-Constraints (5-Iterations)
4. Solve-Bending-Constraints (3-Iterations)
5. Solve-Collision-Constraints (2-Iterations)
6. Solve-Self-Collision (1-Iteration if-Enabled)
7. Update-Visual-Mesh

**PERFORMANCE-BUDGET:**
- LOD-0 (0-10m): 0.5ms-per-Character (full-Simulation 5.000-Strands)
- LOD-1 (10-25m): 0.2ms (simplified-1.000-Strands)
- LOD-2 (25m+): 0ms (no-Physics hair-Animated-with-Bone)


### HAIR-RENDERING-SHADER-SYSTEM

**ANISOTROPIC-SHADING (Kajiya-Kay-Model-Extended):**

**PRINCIPLE:**
Hair-Reflects-Light-Differently-Along-Length vs-Across-Width. Creates-Characteristic-Elongated-Highlights.

**TANGENT-VECTOR:**
- Per-Vertex: Calculate-Direction-Along-Hair-Strand
- Formula: Tangent = (Next-Vertex-Position minus Previous-Vertex-Position) normalized
- Smooth-Transition: Average-with-Neighbors for-Smooth-Highlight

**PRIMARY-SPECULAR (R-Lobe):**
- Light-Reflects-off-Surface-of-Hair
- Formula: Specular = pow(dot(Light Reflect(View Tangent)) roughness) √ó Intensity
- Color: White-ish (reflects-Light-Color)
- Shift: -10-Degrees-Toward-Root (realistic-Cuticle-Angle)
- Width: 5-Degrees (narrow-Highlight)

**SECONDARY-SPECULAR (TT-Lobe):**
- Light-Transmits-Through-Hair exits-Other-Side
- Formula: Similar-to-Primary but-Shifted plus-15-Degrees
- Color: Tinted-by-Hair-Color (light-Passes-Through)
- Width: 10-Degrees (wider-Highlight)
- Intensity: 0.5-of-Primary (less-Bright)

**TERTIARY-SPECULAR (TRT-Lobe):**
- Light-Bounces-Inside-Hair (complex-Path)
- Only-Visible-in-Ultra-Quality
- Shift: Plus-30-Degrees
- Width: 15-Degrees
- Intensity: 0.2-of-Primary

**DIFFUSE-SCATTERING:**
- Base-Hair-Color: Defined-per-Character (blonde brown black red)
- Wrap-Lighting: Light-Wraps-Around-Thin-Strands
- Formula: Diffuse = dot(Normal Light) √ó 0.5 plus 0.5 (double-Sided)

**MULTI-SCATTERING-APPROXIMATION:**
- Problem: Light-Bounces-Multiple-Times-Within-Hair-Volume
- Solution: Add-Ambient-Term-Based-on-Density
- Formula: Ambient = Hair-Color √ó 0.3 √ó (1 minus Density)
- Result: Inner-Hair looks-Softer outer-Hair-more-Defined

**TRANSLUCENCY (Backscatter):**
- When-Light-Behind-Hair: Some-Light-Passes-Through
- Formula: Translucency = pow(dot(minus-View Light) 2) √ó Thickness-Inverse
- Color: Orange-Tint (realistic-Flesh-Tone-Through-Hair)
- Intensity: 0.4
- Example: Backlit-Hair glows-Around-Edges

**OPACITY-MAPPING:**
- Hair-Edges: Alpha-Blend to-Avoid-Hard-Cutoff
- Alpha-Test: Threshold-0.5 (discard-Pixels-Below)
- Dithering: Ordered-Dither-Pattern for-Soft-Edges
- Anti-Aliasing: Supersampling-at-Hair-Edges (expensive but-Necessary)

**LOD-SHADER-VARIANTS:**

**LOD-0-SHADER (0-10m):**
- All-Lobes-Enabled: Primary Secondary Tertiary
- Multi-Scattering: Full-Calculation
- Translucency: Enabled
- Self-Shadowing: Enabled (deep-Shadow-Maps)
- Cost: 2.5ms-per-Character

**LOD-1-SHADER (10-25m):**
- Primary-and-Secondary-Only
- Multi-Scattering: Simplified
- Translucency: Disabled
- Self-Shadowing: Disabled
- Cost: 0.8ms

**LOD-2-SHADER (25m+):**
- Primary-Only
- Multi-Scattering: Disabled
- Translucency: Disabled
- Hair-Rendered-as-Textured-Cards
- Cost: 0.2ms

---

## CMP-PHASE-5: SKIN-SHADER-SYSTEM

### SUBSURFACE-SCATTERING-COMPLETE

**SSS-THEORY:**
Light-Enters-Skin does-Not-Reflect-Immediately but-Scatters-Inside-Then-Exits. Creates-Soft-Glowing-Effect.

**SCATTERING-PROFILE (RGB-Channels):**

**RED-CHANNEL (Deep-Scattering):**
- Penetration-Depth: 1.5mm
- Color: RGB(255 0 0) pure-Red
- Contribution: 40-Percent-of-Total-SSS
- Effect: Visible-in-Ears nose-Fingers (thin-Parts)

**GREEN-CHANNEL (Medium-Scattering):**
- Penetration-Depth: 0.8mm
- Color: RGB(0 255 0) pure-Green
- Contribution: 35-Percent
- Effect: General-Skin-Softness

**BLUE-CHANNEL (Shallow-Scattering):**
- Penetration-Depth: 0.5mm
- Color: RGB(0 0 255) pure-Blue
- Contribution: 25-Percent
- Effect: Surface-Detail-Retention

**SSS-RADIUS-MAP:**
- Texture-Input: Grayscale-Map defines-Where-SSS-Strong
- White-Areas: Full-SSS (ears nose eyelids)
- Gray-Areas: Moderate-SSS (cheeks forehead)
- Black-Areas: Minimal-SSS (bones hard-Structures)

**THICKNESS-MAP:**
- Purpose: Defines-How-Much-Light-Passes-Through
- Measurement: Skin-Thickness-in-Millimeters
- Values:
  - Ears: 1mm (very-Thin)
  - Nose-Wings: 1.5mm
  - Cheeks: 3mm
  - Forehead: 4mm
  - Jaw: 5mm (thickest)
- Backscatter-Effect: Thin-Areas glow-When-Backlit

**SSS-IMPLEMENTATION-METHOD:**

**TEXTURE-SPACE-DIFFUSION:**
- Render-Character-to-2D-Texture (unwrapped-UV)
- Apply-Blur-in-Texture-Space (separate-RGB-Channels different-Blur-Radius)
- Re-Project-onto-3D-Model
- Cost: 1.5ms-per-Character

**SCREEN-SPACE-SSS (Fallback):**
- Blur-in-Screen-Space (cheaper)
- Less-Accurate but-Faster
- Cost: 0.5ms

**CURVATURE-BASED-SSS:**
- Calculate-Surface-Curvature
- Concave-Areas (eye-Sockets): More-SSS
- Convex-Areas (nose-Tip): Less-SSS
- Formula: SSS-Strength = 0.5 plus 0.5 √ó Curvature

### SKIN-MICRO-DETAIL-SYSTEM

**PORE-DETAIL-NORMAL-MAP:**

**RESOLUTION:** 8192x8192 for-Hero-Characters (8K)
**CONTENT:**
- Pore-Pattern: 0.1mm-to-0.3mm-Diameter-Indentations
- Density: ~100-Pores-per-cm¬≤ on-Nose ~30-per-cm¬≤-on-Forehead
- Depth: 0.05mm-to-0.1mm (encoded-in-Normal-Map-Blue-Channel)
- Distribution: Procedurally-Generated-with-Poisson-Disk-Sampling (even-Spacing)

**GENERATION-METHOD:**
- Start-with-Base-Skin-Texture
- Generate-Random-Pore-Locations (avoid-Clumping)
- For-Each-Pore:
  - Add-Circular-Indentation
  - Normal-Vector-Points-Inward
  - Size-Varies-Slightly (0.8-to-1.2-of-Base)
- Blur-Slightly for-Realism (pores-Not-Perfect-Circles)

**WRINKLE-NORMAL-MAP (Expression-Driven):**

**STATIC-WRINKLES:**
- Age-Lines: Forehead-Lines crow's-Feet laugh-Lines
- Always-Visible (baked-into-Base-Normal)
- Depth: 0.2mm-to-0.5mm

**DYNAMIC-WRINKLES:**
- Compression-Wrinkles: Appear-When-Muscle-Contracts
- Example: Frown-Lines-Appear-When-browDown-Blendshape-Active
- Implementation:
  - 20-Separate-Wrinkle-Normal-Maps (one-per-Major-Expression)
  - Blend-Based-on-Blendshape-Weight
  - Formula: Final-Normal = Base-Normal lerp Wrinkle-Normal √ó Blendshape-Weight

**WRINKLE-MAPS-LIST:**
1. Forehead-Horizontal-Lines (browUp)
2. Glabella-Vertical-Lines (browDown angry)
3. Crow's-Feet (eyeSquint smile)
4. Nasolabial-Folds (smile)
5. Marionette-Lines (frown)
6. Bunny-Lines (nose-Wrinkle)
7. Neck-Bands (tension)
8. etc.

**VEIN-VISIBILITY-MAP:**

**DISTRIBUTION:**
- Temples: Visible-Blue-Green-Veins
- Eyelids: Very-Thin-Skin shows-Veins
- Hands: Veins-on-Back-of-Hand
- Forehead: Subtle-Veins (more-Visible-when-Angry)

**RENDERING:**
- Subsurface-Color: Bluish-Tint (deoxygenated-Blood)
- Depth: 1-2mm-Below-Surface
- Thickness: 0.5mm-to-2mm-Diameter
- Visibility-Map: Grayscale-Texture (white = visible-Vein)

**BLENDING:**
- Mix-Vein-Color-with-Skin-Based-on-Thickness-Map
- Formula: Final-Color = Skin-Color lerp Vein-Color √ó Vein-Visibility √ó (1 minus Thickness)

**FRECKLES-MOLES-SCARS:**

**DETAIL-MASK-TEXTURE:**
- Resolution: 4096x4096
- Alpha-Channel: Stores-Detail-Locations
- RGB-Channels: Store-Detail-Colors

**FRECKLES:**
- Size: 1-3-Pixels-in-Texture (0.5mm-to-1mm-in-World)
- Color: Darker-Than-Skin by-20-Percent
- Distribution: Concentrated-on-Nose-Cheeks (sun-Exposed-Areas)
- Count: 50-200-per-Character (varies)

**MOLES:**
- Size: 5-10-Pixels (2mm-to-5mm)
- Color: Dark-Brown-to-Black
- 3D-Geometry: Optional-Raised-Bump (50-Polygons)
- Count: 5-15-per-Character

**SCARS:**
- Linear-or-Irregular-Shapes
- Color: Lighter-Than-Skin or-Reddish
- Normal-Map-Depression: Scar-Tissue-Different-Texture
- Examples: Facial-Scar forehead-Cut eyebrow-Notch

### SKIN-WETNESS-SYSTEM

**SWEAT-ACCUMULATION-ZONES:**

**HIGH-SWEAT-AREAS:**
- Forehead: 100-Percent-Sweat-Coverage
- Nose: 80-Percent
- Upper-Lip: 60-Percent
- Temples: 70-Percent

**MEDIUM-SWEAT-AREAS:**
- Cheeks: 30-Percent
- Chin: 40-Percent
- Neck: 50-Percent

**LOW-SWEAT-AREAS:**
- Rest-of-Body: 10-20-Percent

**SWEAT-TRIGGER-CONDITIONS:**
- Physical-Exertion: Running-Fighting increases-Sweat
- Temperature: Hot-Environment increases-Sweat
- Stress: High-Tension-Situations trigger-Stress-Sweat
- Time: Accumulates-Over-Time capped-at-Maximum

**WETNESS-SHADER-PROPERTIES:**

**DRY-SKIN (Wetness-0.0):**
- Roughness: 0.6 (matte-Finish)
- Specular: 0.4 (low-Reflection)

**WET-SKIN (Wetness-1.0):**
- Roughness: 0.1 (very-Smooth glossy)
- Specular: 0.9 (high-Reflection)
- Darkening: Base-Color √ó 0.8 (wet-Looks-Darker)

**TRANSITION:**
- Linear-Interpolation-Based-on-Wetness-Value
- Formula: Final-Roughness = Dry-Roughness lerp Wet-Roughness √ó Wetness

**DRIP-ANIMATION:**

**WATER-DROPLET-PARTICLES:**
- Spawn-on-High-Sweat-Areas (forehead nose)
- Initial-Position: Random-Point-on-Skin
- Movement: Follow-Gravity-Plus-Surface-Flow
- Path: Flows-Down-Face following-Contours
- Speed: 2cm-per-Second
- Lifetime: 3-5-Seconds then-Disappears

**DROPLET-MESH:**
- Polygon-Count: 20-Triangles-per-Droplet
- Shape: Elongated-Teardrop
- Shader: Highly-Reflective-Transparent
- Max-Active-Droplets: 10-per-Character

**DRYING-OVER-TIME:**
- Sweat-Evaporates-Gradually
- Rate: Minus-0.1-Wetness-per-Second
- Accelerated-by: Wind-Movement
- Result: Skin-Returns-to-Dry-State after-10-Seconds

## CMP-PHASE-6: CLOTHING-SYSTEM-COMPLETE

### MULTI-LAYER-CLOTHING-ARCHITECTURE

**PROPERTIES:**

### CLOTHING-PHYSICS-SYSTEM

**CLOTH-VS-BODY-COLLISION:**

**BODY-COLLISION-PRIMITIVES:**
- Head: 1-Sphere radius-10cm
- Neck: 1-Capsule length-8cm radius-4cm
- Torso: 2-Capsules (upper-Torso lower-Torso)
- Arms: 2-Capsules-each-Arm (upper-Arm forearm)
- Legs: 2-Capsules-each-Leg (thigh calf)
- Total: 15-Collision-Primitives

**COLLISION-DETECTION:**
- Per-Cloth-Vertex: Check-Distance-to-Each-Primitive
- If-Inside-Primitive: Push-Vertex-Outside
- Method: Project-onto-Capsule-Surface
- Cost: 0.2ms-per-Character

**CLOTH-VS-CLOTH-COLLISION:**

**MULTI-LAYER-INTERACTIONS:**
- Shirt-vs-Jacket: Jacket-Over-Shirt (outer-Layer-Priority)
- Jacket-vs-Scarf: Scarf-Hangs-Outside
- Belt-vs-Shirt: Shirt-Tucks-Into-Belt

**COLLISION-LAYERS:**
- Layer-0 (Underwear): Collides-with-Body-Only
- Layer-1 (Shirt): Collides-with-Body-and-Layer-0
- Layer-2 (Jacket): Collides-with-Body-Layer-0-Layer-1
- Layer-3 (Accessories): Collides-with-All

**FRICTION-MODEL:**
- Cotton-on-Cotton: Friction-0.5 (moderate-Slide)
- Leather-on-Cotton: Friction-0.6 (more-Grip)
- Polyester-on-Polyester: Friction-0.3 (slippery)

**BUTTON-AND-ZIPPER-CONSTRAINTS:**

**BUTTON-MECHANICS:**
- Button-Position: Fixed-to-Button-Hole
- Buttonhole-Edge: Cannot-Pass-Through
- When-Buttoned: Two-Fabric-Edges-Pulled-Together
- When-Unbuttoned: Fabric-Separates freely-Flaps

**ZIPPER-MECHANICS:**
- Zipper-Teeth: Discrete-Steps (not-Smooth-Slide)
- Zipper-Slider: Moves-from-Bottom-to-Top
- Zipper-State: 0-Percent (fully-Open) to-100-Percent (fully-Closed)
- Fabric-Behavior: Closed-Zipper-Tight open-Zipper-Flaps

**ANIMATION-SYSTEM:**
- Open-Zipper-Animation: 1-Second-Duration (hand-Pulls-Slider-Up)
- Button-Animation: 0.5-Seconds-per-Button (sequential)

**POCKET-DEFORMATION:**

**EMPTY-POCKET:**
- Flat-Against-Body
- Subtle-Stitching-Detail

**FILLED-POCKET:**
- Bulge-Outward
- Deformation-Based-on-Item-Size
- Example: Phone-in-Pocket (5cm-Bulge rectangular-Shape)
- Weight: Pocket-Sags-Downward-Slightly

**PHYSICS-SIMULATION:**
- Add-Mass-to-Pocket-Vertices
- Gravity-Pulls-Down
- Cloth-Stretches-Around-Object

### CLOTHING-MATERIAL-SPECIFICATIONS

**FABRIC-TYPE-1-COTTON:**
- Roughness: 0.7
- Specular: 0.3
- Texture: Fine-Weave visible-at-Close-Range
- Wrinkle-Tendency: High (wrinkles-Easily)
- Stretch: Low (minimal-Elasticity)
- Wind-Response: Moderate

**FABRIC-TYPE-2-WOOL:**
- Roughness: 0.8 (very-Matte)
- Specular: 0.2
- Texture: Fuzzy-Surface micro-Fibers
- Wrinkle-Tendency: Low (resists-Wrinkles)
- Stretch: Low
- Wind-Response: Low (heavy-Fabric)

**FABRIC-TYPE-3-LEATHER:**
- Roughness: 0.4-to-0.6 (depends-on-Finish)
- Specular: 0.6 (shiny-Highlights)
- Texture: Grain-Pattern pores
- Wrinkle-Tendency: Low (stiff-Material)
- Stretch: None
- Wind-Response: None (rigid)
- Normal-Map: Detailed-Grain-Texture-4K

**FABRIC-TYPE-4-POLYESTER:**
- Roughness: 0.3 (smooth-Shiny)
- Specular: 0.7
- Texture: Smooth-Almost-Plastic-Like
- Wrinkle-Tendency: Very-Low (wrinkle-Resistant)
- Stretch: Medium
- Wind-Response: High (light-Flutters)

**FABRIC-TYPE-5-DENIM:**
- Roughness: 0.6
- Specular: 0.4
- Texture: Twill-Weave diagonal-Pattern
- Wrinkle-Tendency: Medium
- Stretch: Low (unless-Stretch-Denim)
- Wind-Response: Low (thick-Heavy)
- Color: Fades-with-Wear (wear-Map-Texture)

**WETNESS-RESPONSE-PER-MATERIAL:**

**COTTON-WET:**
- Absorption: High (soaks-Up-Water)
- Darkening: 50-Percent-Darker
- Roughness-Change: 0.7 to-0.3 (becomes-Shinier)
- Weight-Increase: 2x (heavier-when-Wet)
- Drying-Time: 5-Minutes-Gameplay-Time

**LEATHER-WET:**
- Absorption: Low (water-Beads-on-Surface)
- Darkening: 30-Percent
- Roughness-Change: 0.5 to-0.2 (very-Shiny)
- Weight-Increase: 1.2x
- Drying-Time: 2-Minutes

**POLYESTER-WET:**
- Absorption: Very-Low (water-Runs-Off)
- Darkening: 10-Percent
- Roughness-Change: Minimal
- Weight-Increase: 1.1x
- Drying-Time: 30-Seconds

- C: "Ver√§nderung-dauert-Zeit." ‚Üí Patience

- If-Reputation-High: Plus-20-Percent-Success-Chance
- If-Reputation-Low: Minus-20-Percent

### QUEST-5: "VIP-EVAKUIERUNG"

**QUEST-OVERVIEW:**
Rescue-High-Value-Target from-Danger-Zone escort-Mission under-Fire.

**TRIGGER:**

  - Melee-Attackers: 10-NPCs with-Sticks-Bottles

  - Flanking-Attack from-Alley
  - Molotov-Cocktails thrown

- Wave-3 (Near-Stephansplatz): 10-Elite-Extremists
  - Organized-Attackers with-Makeshift-Weapons
  - Focus-Fire-on-VIP
  - Player-Must: Use-Riot-Shield-or-Call-Backup

**TIME-LIMIT:** 10-Minutes total-Escort
**DIFFICULTY-MODIFIERS:**
- Night-Time: Reduced-Visibility
- Rain: Slippery-Ground slower-Movement
- High-Tension: More-Aggressive-NPCs

**OUTCOMES:**

- Wagner-Thanks-Player: "Sie-haben-mir-das-Leben-gerettet!"

- Achievement-"Leibw√§chter"
- Story-Consequence: Wagner-Supports-M√ºller politically-Later

**SUCCESS (VIP-Injured):**
- Wagner-Wounded-but-Alive: Bullet-Graze or-Hit-by-Stone
- Medic-Treatment-Required
- Reputation-Plus-10
- Achievement-"Schutzengel"

**FAILURE (VIP-Killed):**
- Wagner-Dies: Headshot-or-Beaten-to-Death
- Massive-Political-Fallout
- Reputation-Minus-30
- Tension-Plus-40
- Achievement-"Katastrophales-Versagen"
- Possible-Game-Over (depending-on-Difficulty)

### QUEST-6: "BOMBENDROHUNG"

**QUEST-OVERVIEW:**

- Method: Phone-Call to-Police-HQ
- Caller: Distorted-Voice "Bombe-explodiert-in-30-Minuten"

**SEARCH-LOCATIONS (10-Possible-Sites):**
1. Stephansdom-Interior (Cathedral)
2. U-Bahn-Station-U1
3. Haas-Haus-Ground-Floor

- K9-Unit: Police-Dog-can-Sniff (if-Called-as-Backup)
- Civilian-Reports: NPCs-may-Report-Suspicious-Package

**BOMB-APPEARANCE:**
- Package: Cardboard-Box 30cm√ó20cm√ó15cm
- Wires: Visible-Red-Blue-Green-Wires-through-Gaps
- Timer: Digital-Display counting-Down
- Fake-or-Real: 50-Percent-Chance-it's-a-Hoax

**INSPECTION:**
- X-Ray-Scanner: Portable-Device shows-Internal-Components
- Expert-Opinion: Call-Bomb-Squad-Specialist (radio-Advice)
- Visual-Clues:
  - Real-Bomb: C4-Explosive-Visible battery-Connected professional-Wiring
  - Fake-Bomb: Clay-or-Playdough batteries-Not-Connected amateur-Setup

**DECISION:**
- Option-A-Defuse: Attempt-Manual-Defusal (if-Real dangerous)
- Option-B-Evacuate: Clear-Area-and-Let-Bomb-Squad-Handle
- Option-C-Ignore: If-Determined-Fake (risky-if-Wrong)

**OBJECTIVE-3: Defuse-Bomb (5-Minutes):**
**DEFUSAL-MINIGAME:**
- Wire-Cutting-Puzzle: 3-Wires (Red-Blue-Green)
- Correct-Sequence: Determined-by-Clues
- Clues-Found:
  - Clue-1-Battery-Type: "Red-Wire-Connected-to-Positive"
  - Clue-2-Timer-Model: "Green-Wire-is-Ground"
  - Clue-3-Expert-Advice: "Cut-Blue-Last"
- Correct-Order: Red ‚Üí Green ‚Üí Blue
- Wrong-Cut: Explosion-Triggered

**TENSION-MECHANIC:**
- Timer-Visible: Counts-Down on-Screen
- Heart-Rate-Sound: Intensifies-as-Time-Runs-Out
- Hands-Shake: Cursor-Wobbles (makes-Clicking-Harder)

**OUTCOMES:**

**SUCCESS-DEFUSED:**
- Bomb-Disabled-with-5-Seconds-Remaining
- Crowd-Cheers
- Reputation-Plus-25
- Achievement-"Bombenentsch√§rfer"
- Tension-Minus-20 (people-Feel-Safe)

**SUCCESS-EVACUATED:**
- Area-Cleared bomb-Squad-Arrives
- Controlled-Detonation (if-Real) or-Removal (if-Fake)
- Reputation-Plus-10
- Achievement-"Vorsichtig"
- No-Casualties

**FAILURE-WRONG-WIRE:**
- Explosion-Occurs
- 10-50-NPCs-Killed (depending-on-Evacuation)
- Player-Injured-or-Killed
- Reputation-Minus-50
- Tension-Plus-50
- Achievement-"Fatale-Entscheidung"
- Possible-Game-Over

**HOAX-DETECTED:**
- Bomb-is-Fake
- Reputation-Plus-5 (for-Handling-Threat)

- Achievement-"Falscher-Alarm"

- Personality: Aggressive-Short-Temper
- Status: Currently-on-Duty-at-Stephansplatz

**EVIDENCE-PRESENTATION:**
- Show-Video: Berger-Visible-Shooting
- Berger-Reaction: "Das-war-Notwehr! Er-griff-nach-meiner-Waffe!"
- Contradiction: Video-Shows-Victim-Running-Away not-Attacking

**TRUTH-REVEALED:**
Berger-Breaks-Down: "Er-beschimpfte-mich... ich-verlor-die-Beherrschung..."
Admission: Intentional-Shooting anger-Not-Self-Defense

**DECISION:**

**OPTION-A: ARREST-BERGER (Justice):**
- Handcuff-Berger take-to-Custody
- Charge: Manslaughter-or-Murder
- Trial: Berger-Convicted sentenced
- Consequences:
  - Justice-Served victim's-Family-Satisfied
  - Police-Morale-Drops (officers-Feel-Betrayed)
  - Public-Trust-Increases (accountability)
- Reputation: Plus-15-with-Public minus-10-with-Police
- Achievement-"Gerechter-Richter"

**OPTION-B: COVER-UP (Protect-Police):**
- Destroy-Video-Evidence
- Threaten-Witnesses-to-Silence
- File-Report: "Victim-Armed-Self-Defense-Justified"
- Consequences:
  - Berger-Goes-Free continues-Duty
  - Corruption-Deepens
  - If-Truth-Leaks-Later: Massive-Scandal M√ºller-Implicated
- Reputation: Plus-10-with-Police minus-30-with-Public (if-Discovered)
- Achievement-"Komplize"
- Moral-Weight: Heavy (haunts-Player)

**OPTION-C: COMPROMISE (Forced-Resignation):**
- Make-Deal-with-Berger: "Resign-Quietly no-Charges."
- Berger-Agrees: Leaves-Force
- Victim's-Family-Compensated: Hush-Money
- Consequences:
  - Justice-Partially-Served (Berger-Gone but-Not-Punished)
  - Public-Unaware (no-Scandal)
  - Uneasy-Peace

### QUEST-9: "BRENNENDE-BARRIKADE"

**QUEST-OVERVIEW:**
Fire-Spreading-from-Barricade civilians-Trapped rescue-Mission.

- Event: Molotov-Cocktail-Thrown-at-Barricade
- Fire-Starts: Rapidly-Spreads to-Adjacent-Building

**FIRE-SPECS:**
- Origin: Wooden-Barricade (tables-chairs-pallets)
- Size: 5-Meters-Diameter growing-1-Meter-per-Minute
- Spread-Path: Building-Facade (timber-Frame-burns-Fast)
- Wind: Strong-West-to-East (accelerates-Spread)
- Trapped-Civilians: 8-People-Inside-Building (2nd-Floor)

**BUILDING-DETAILS:**
- Type: Old-Gr√ºnderzeit-Building (1890s)
- Construction: Timber-Frame-with-Plaster
- Exits: Main-Door (blocked-by-Fire) back-Exit (locked)
- Windows: 2nd-Floor-windows-6-Meters-High (jump-Dangerous)

**OBJECTIVE-2: Extinguish-Fire (10-Minutes):**
**FIREFIGHTING-OPTIONS:**

**OPTION-A: WATER-CANNON:**
- Equipment: Police-Water-Cannon-Truck (Wasserwerfer)
- Effectiveness: High (1000-Liters-per-Minute)
- Time-to-Setup: 3-Minutes (drive-to-Location aim-Nozzle)
- Side-Effect: Water-Damage-to-Building
- Success-Rate: 90-Percent

**OPTION-B: FIRE-EXTINGUISHERS:**
- Equipment: Handheld-CO2-Extinguishers (5-Available)
- Effectiveness: Low (small-Fires-only)
- Time: 5-Minutes (multiple-Officers-needed)
- Risk: Close-Proximity-to-Fire (burn-Danger)
- Success-Rate: 40-Percent

**OPTION-C: CALL-FIRE-BRIGADE:**
- Response-Time: 8-Minutes-ETA
- Effectiveness: Very-High (professional-Equipment)
- Risk: Delay-may-be-Too-Long (civilians-Die)
- Success-Rate: 95-Percent (if-They-Arrive-in-Time)

**FIRE-SPREAD-MECHANIC:**
- Every-Minute: Fire-Grows-20-Percent
- After-5-Minutes: Entire-Building-Engulfed
- After-10-Minutes: Structural-Collapse (building-Destroyed)

**OBJECTIVE-3: Rescue-Civilians (8-Minutes):**
**RESCUE-METHODS:**

**METHOD-A: LADDER-RESCUE:**
- Equipment: Fire-Ladder (8-Meters)
- Setup-Time: 2-Minutes
- Capacity: 1-Person-per-Minute
- Total-Time: 10-Minutes (too-Slow for-8-People)
- Risk: Ladder-may-Break-if-Fire-Weakens-Wall

**METHOD-B: WINDOW-JUMP (Cushioned-Landing):**
- Equipment: Firefighter-Jump-Sheet (4-Officers-Hold)
- Jump-Height: 6-Meters
- Risk: Injury-Possible (broken-Bones)
- Speed: All-8-People-in-3-Minutes
- Success-Rate: 80-Percent-Unharmed 20-Percent-Injured

**METHOD-C: BREAK-DOWN-BACK-DOOR:**
- Equipment: Battering-Ram or-Crowbar
- Time: 4-Minutes-to-Force-Open
- Path: Through-Smoke-filled-Hallway
- Risk: Smoke-Inhalation
- Requires: Breathing-Masks (if-Available)

**SIMULTANEOUS-ACTIONS:**
- Team-A: Fights-Fire (choose-Option-A-B-or-C)
- Team-B: Rescues-Civilians (choose-Method-A-B-or-C)
- Player: Coordinates-Both (split-Attention)

**OUTCOMES:**

**FULL-SUCCESS:**
- Fire-Extinguished-Before-Spread
- All-8-Civilians-Rescued-Unharmed
- Reputation-Plus-30
- Achievement-"Feuerwehrmann"
- Media-Headline: "Polizei-Rettet-Leben"

**PARTIAL-SUCCESS:**
- Fire-Contained civilians-Rescued-but-Some-Injured
- Reputation-Plus-15
- Achievement-"Lebensretter"
- 2-4-Civilians-Injured (burns-or-Broken-Bones)

**FAILURE:**
- Fire-Spreads-Out-of-Control
- Building-Collapses
- 3-8-Civilians-Killed (depending-on-Rescue-Efforts)
- Reputation-Minus-20
- Achievement-"Tragisches-Versagen"
- Media-Headline: "Polizei-Versagt-bei-Rettung"

**COLLATERAL-DAMAGE:**
- Adjacent-Buildings: May-Catch-Fire (spreads-Further)
- Economic-Loss: Historical-Building-Destroyed
- Tension-Increase: Plus-15 (fear-of-Fire)

### QUEST-6: "BOMBENDROHUNG"

**QUEST-OVERVIEW:**

- Clear-Zone: 100-Meter-Radius-from-Suspected-Location
- NPC-Reaction: Panic-Stampede
- Player-Actions:

**SEARCH-LOCATIONS:**

4. **Behind-Newspaper-Stand:** Cardboard-Box

10. **Dom-Entrance-Steps:** Hidden-in-Shadows

- Visual-Search: Player-Walks-Around-Inspects
- Bomb-Dog: Call-K9-Unit (if-Available reduces-Search-Time)
- Metal-Detector: Scan-for-Electronic-Components
- Civilian-Tips: NPCs-Report-Suspicious-Items

**BOMB-IDENTIFICATION:**
- Real-Bomb-Clues:
  - Ticking-Sound (audible-within-2-Meters)
  - Wires-Visible (red green blue)
  - LED-Timer-Display (shows-Countdown)
  - Weight: 5-Kilograms (heavy-for-Size)

**OBJECTIVE-3: Defuse-Bomb (5-Minutes-Remaining):**

**BOMB-DEFUSAL-MINIGAME:**

**BOMB-COMPONENTS:**
- Timer-Display: Digital-Countdown
- Power-Source: 9V-Battery
- Detonator: Blasting-Cap
- Explosive: C4-Plastic-Explosive (2-kg)
- Wiring: 4-Wires (Red Blue Green Yellow)
- Trigger: Pressure-Plate (anti-Tamper)

**DEFUSAL-OPTIONS:**

**OPTION-A: CUT-WIRE (50-Percent-Success):**
- Instructions: "Cut-Blue-Wire to-Disable-Timer"
- Problem: Which-Wire-is-Correct?
- Wire-Colors: Red Blue Green Yellow
- Hint-System: Call-Bomb-Squad-Expert (phone-Guide)
- Expert-Says: "Based-on-Description... Try-Blue-Wire."
- Risk: Wrong-Wire-Instant-Detonation

**WIRE-PUZZLE:**
- Correct-Wire: Blue (disables-Timer)
- Red-Wire: Decoy (cuts-Power but-Triggers-Backup-Timer)
- Green-Wire: Dummy (does-Nothing)
- Yellow-Wire: Instant-Detonation

**OPTION-B: REMOVE-BATTERY (30-Percent-Success):**
- Method: Disconnect-Power-Source
- Problem: Anti-Tamper-Switch
- If-Moved-Wrong: Triggers-Detonation
- Requires: Steady-Hands (mini-Game steady-Cursor)

**OPTION-C: FREEZE-BOMB (70-Percent-Success):**
- Method: Liquid-Nitrogen-Spray (if-Available)
- Effect: Freezes-Electronics prevents-Detonation
- Time: 2-Minutes-to-Apply
- Drawback: Requires-Special-Equipment (must-Call-Bomb-Squad)

**OPTION-D: EVACUATE-FURTHER (Safe-but-Fails-Quest):**
- Decision: "Too-Risky. Everyone-Back-200-Meters!"
- Result: Bomb-Explodes (no-Casualties but-Property-Damage)
- Consequence: Media-Criticizes-Police Quest-Failed

**DEFUSAL-OUTCOME:**

**SUCCESS:**
- Wire-Cut: Timer-Stops-at-00:03 (dramatic)
- Relief: "Wir-haben-es-geschafft..."
- Bomb-Squad-Arrives: Takes-Bomb-for-Analysis
- Reward: Reputation-Plus-25 Achievement-"Bombentechniker"
- Investigation: Trace-Bomb-to-Extremist-Group

**FAILURE:**
- Explosion: Massive-Blast-Radius
- Casualties: 0 (area-Evacuated) but-Buildings-Damaged
- Media: "Polizei-Versagt-bei-Bombenentsch√§rfung"
- Reputation: Minus-30
- Tension: Increases-to-95-Percent (city-in-Panic)

**TWIST-OPTION:**
- Bomb-is-Fake: Open-Box find-Note "Nur-ein-Test. Ihr-seid-nicht-bereit."
- Result: Relief-but-Anger
- Consequence: Wasted-Resources Quest-Complete-but-No-Reward

**OBJECTIVE-2: Fire-Suppression (5-Minutes):**

**FIREFIGHTING-OPTIONS:**

**OPTION-A: WATER-CANNON-TRUCK:**
- Equipment: Wasserwerfer-3000 (police-Truck)
- Specs: 1200-Liters-per-Minute 60-Meter-Range
- Setup-Time: 2-Minutes (drive-from-Stephansplatz)
- Effectiveness: Extinguishes-Fire-in-3-Minutes
- Side-Effect: Water-Damage (minor)
- Success-Rate: 95-Percent

**OPTION-B: FIRE-EXTINGUISHERS:**
- Equipment: 8-Handheld-CO2-Extinguishers
- Capacity: 5kg-Each (40kg-Total)
- Range: 3-Meters
- Effectiveness: Only-for-Small-Fires
- Time: 6-Minutes (too-Slow)
- Success-Rate: 20-Percent
- Risk: Officers-Get-Too-Close (burns)

**OPTION-C: FIRE-BRIGADE:**
- Response-Time: 6-Minutes-ETA
- Equipment: Professional-Fire-Trucks-2-Units
- Effectiveness: Complete-Suppression
- Problem: May-Arrive-Too-Late
- Success-Rate: 90-Percent (if-No-Delay)

**OBJECTIVE-3: Rescue-Trapped-Civilians (Parallel):**

**RESCUE-METHODS:**

**METHOD-A: FIRE-ESCAPE-LADDER:**
- Location: West-Side-of-Building
- Accessibility: Clear (no-Fire-Yet)
- Capacity: 1-Person-per-30-Seconds
- Total-Time: 6-Minutes for-12-People
- Risk: LOW
- Requires: Guide-People-to-Ladder

**METHOD-B: AERIAL-LADDER-TRUCK:**
- Equipment: Fire-Brigade-Ladder (30m-Height)
- Availability: With-Fire-Brigade (6-Minute-Wait)
- Capacity: 2-People-per-Minute
- Total-Time: 6-Minutes after-Arrival
- Risk: MEDIUM (exposed-to-Smoke)

**METHOD-C: INTERIOR-EVACUATION:**
- Path: Through-Smoke-Filled-Stairwell
- Equipment: Breathing-Masks (6-Available)
- Requires: Officers-Enter-Building
- Risk: HIGH (smoke-Inhalation)
- Time: 4-Minutes (fast-but-Dangerous)
- Casualties: Possible-Officer-Injuries

**COORDINATION-CHALLENGE:**
Player-Must-Manage-2-Teams-Simultaneously:
- **Team-Alpha:** Fights-Fire (choose-Option)
- **Team-Bravo:** Rescues-Civilians (choose-Method)

**TIME-PRESSURE:**
- Minute-0: Fire-Starts
- Minute-2: Fire-Reaches-Building
- Minute-4: Smoke-Enters-Apartments
- Minute-6: People-Overcome-by-Smoke
- Minute-8: Building-Collapses

**OUTCOMES:**

**PERFECT-RESCUE:**
- Fire-Extinguished-in-3-Minutes
- All-12-Civilians-Rescued-Unharmed
- No-Structural-Damage
- Reputation: Plus-30
- Achievement: "Feuerwehrheld"
- Media: "Polizei-Rettet-Familie!"

**PARTIAL-SUCCESS:**
- Fire-Contained
- 10-Civilians-Rescued 2-Injured (smoke-Inhalation)
- Building-Damaged-but-Standing
- Reputation: Plus-15
- Achievement: "Lebensretter"

**FAILURE:**
- Fire-Out-of-Control
- 4-Civilians-Killed (smoke-or-Burns)
- Building-Collapsed
- Reputation: Minus-25
- Achievement: "Trag√∂die"
- Media: "Polizei-Versagt!"

### QUEST-10: "DER MAULWURF"

**QUEST-OVERVIEW:**
Find-Traitor-Leaking-Police-Intel to-Demonstranten.

- Discovery: Police-Plan-Leaked

- Incident-2: Police-Movement-Predicted ambush-Set
- Incident-3: Classified-Document-Found-on-Demonstrant
- Conclusion: Someone-Inside-Police-is-Informant

**OBJECTIVE-1: Identify-Suspects (5-Minutes):**

**5-POTENTIAL-MAULW√úRFE:**

- Access: ALL-Computer-Systems
- Motive: Money (gambling-Debts-50k-Euros)

- Position: Radio-Dispatcher

- Motive: Ideology (sympathizes-with-Demonstranten)

- Red-Flag: Seen-Texting-During-Classified-Briefing

- Motive: Underpaid (minimum-Wage)
- Alibi: Night-Shift (alone)
- Red-Flag: Spotted-in-Commander's-Office-After-Hours

**SUSPECT-5: Commander's-Secretary-Lisa-Bauer:**
- Position: Administrative-Assistant
- Access: Commander's-Files
- Motive: Romantic-Involvement-with-Demonstrant-Leader
- Alibi: Working-Late (no-Witnesses)
- Red-Flag: Phone-Calls-to-Unknown-Number

**OBJECTIVE-2: Gather-Evidence (20-Minutes):**

- Search-For: Calls-to-Known-Demonstrant-Numbers
- Time: 10-Minutes (IT-Department)
- Result: Schmidt-and-Bauer-Have-Suspicious-Calls

**METHOD-B: COMPUTER-FORENSICS:**
- Scan: Email-Logs file-Access-History
- Search-For: Classified-Files-Accessed-Unusually
- Time: 15-Minutes
- Result: M√ºller-Accessed-Raid-Plans-Outside-Work-Hours

**METHOD-C: PHYSICAL-SURVEILLANCE:**
- Setup: Hidden-Cameras-in-Offices
- Duration: 24-Hours-Monitoring
- Result: Wagner-Photographing-Documents

**METHOD-D: STING-OPERATION:**
- Plan: Feed-False-Intel-to-Each-Suspect (different-Info)
- Monitor: Which-Info-Reaches-Demonstranten
- Time: 6-Hours
- Result: Bauer's-False-Info-Appears-in-Demonstrant-Chat

**OBJECTIVE-3: Confront-Maulwurf:**

**TRAITOR-REVEALED:** Lisa-Bauer (Secretary)

**EVIDENCE:**
- Phone-Records: 47-Calls-to-Martin-Krause (demonstrant-Leader)

- Document-Leak: Photos-of-Classified-Files-Sent-via-WhatsApp
- Motive: Love-and-Ideology

**CONFRONTATION-SCENE:**
- Location: Commander's-Office
- Bauer-Called-In: "Sie-wollten-mich-sprechen?"
- Player-Presents-Evidence

**BAUER'S-CONFESSION:**
Bauer: "Ich-liebe-ihn. Ich-konnte-nicht-zusehen-wie-ihr-ihn-jagt."

**PLAYER-DECISION:**

**OPTION-A: ARREST-BAUER (Justice):**
- Charge: Treason-Espionage
- Trial: 8-Years-Prison
- Krause-Reaction: Devastated (loses-Support)
- Consequences:
  - Leak-Stopped
  - Police-Security-Restored
  - Harsh-Example-Set
- Reputation: Plus-25-Police Plus-10-Public
- Achievement: "Verr√§ter-Gefasst"

**OPTION-B: TURN-DOUBLE-AGENT:**
- Deal: "Work-for-Us. Feed-False-Intel-to-Krause."
- Bauer-Agrees: Becomes-Double-Agent
- Result: Tactical-Advantage (control-Info-Flow)
- Risk: Bauer-May-Betray-Again
- Consequences:
  - Demonstranten-Misled
  - Police-Win-Strategic-Advantage
- Reputation: Plus-30-Police
- Achievement: "Schachmeister"

**OPTION-C: EXILE (Mercy):**
- Deal: "Leave-Vienna. Never-Return."
- Bauer-Accepts: Resigns-and-Disappears
- Krause-Loses-Intel-Source
- Consequences:
  - Leak-Stopped
  - No-Scandal
  - Bauer-Lives-in-Exile
- Reputation: Plus-10-Police
- Achievement: "Gnadenakt"

# üé¨ BRANCHING-MAIN-QUEST-SYSTEM

## MISSION-STRUCTURE-WITH-BRANCH-POINTS

**LINEAR-ACTS:**
- **ACT-1 (0-30min):** Setup arrival-at-Stephansplatz meet-NPCs
- **ACT-2 (30-90min):** Escalation side-Quests reputation-Building
- **ACT-3 (90-150min):** Climax decision-Points
- **ACT-4 (150-180min):** Resolution ending

**5-MAJOR-BRANCH-POINTS:**

### BRANCH-POINT-1 (30-Minute-Mark):

**SITUATION:** Crowd-Becoming-Aggressive

**CHOICE-1A: DIPLOMATIC-APPROACH**
- Action: Announce-Willingness-to-Negotiate
- Effect: Tension-Minus-10
- Opens: Quest-"Das-Ultimatum" (early)
- Path: PEACEFUL-ROUTE

**CHOICE-1B: SHOW-OF-FORCE**
- Action: Deploy-Riot-Police-Intimidate
- Effect: Tension-Plus-15
- Opens: Quest-"Undercover-Infiltration"
- Path: AGGRESSIVE-ROUTE

**CONSEQUENCES:**
- Peaceful-Route: More-Dialog-Options later
- Aggressive-Route: More-Combat-Encounters

---

### BRANCH-POINT-2 (60-Minute-Mark):

**SITUATION:** Demonstranten-Demand-Meeting-with-Krause

**CHOICE-2A: ACCEPT-MEETING**
- Action: Arrange-Face-to-Face-with-Krause
- Effect: Quest-"Das-Ultimatum" triggers
- Outcome: Potential-Peaceful-Resolution
- Path: NEGOTIATION-PATH

**CHOICE-2B: REFUSE-MEETING**
- Action: "No-Negotiation-with-Extremists"
- Effect: Tension-Plus-20
- Outcome: Violence-Escalates
- Path: CONFRONTATION-PATH

---

### BRANCH-POINT-3 (90-Minute-Mark):

**SITUATION:** Violence-Erupts minor-Injuries

**CHOICE-3A: USE-TEAR-GAS**
- Action: Deploy-Chemical-Agents
- Effect: Crowd-Disperses-but-Angry
- Media-Reaction: Negative
- Path: SUPPRESSION-PATH

**CHOICE-3B: ALLOW-PROTEST-TO-CONTINUE**
- Action: Pull-Back-Give-Space
- Effect: Violence-Subsides-Temporarily
- Media-Reaction: Positive
- Path: TOLERANCE-PATH

---

### BRANCH-POINT-4 (120-Minute-Mark):

**SITUATION:** Krause-Calls-for-Storm-on-Rathaus

**CHOICE-4A: ARREST-KRAUSE**
- Action: Raid-and-Capture
- Effect: Demonstranten-Leaderless chaos
- Outcome: Violence-Spikes-Short-Term then-Collapses
- Path: DECAPITATION-PATH

**CHOICE-4B: LET-HIM-SPEAK**
- Action: Allow-Krause-Public-Address
- Effect: Crowd-Listens may-Calm-Down
- Outcome: Depends-on-Speech-Content
- Path: PLATFORM-PATH

---

### BRANCH-POINT-5 (Final-150-Minute-Mark):

**SITUATION:** Endgame-Approaching

**4-FINAL-PATHS (based-on-Previous-Choices):**

**PATH-A: FULL-PEACEFUL-RESOLUTION**
- Requirements: All-Peaceful-Choices reputation-80-Plus
- Outcome: Krause-Agrees-to-End-Demo
- Result: S-RANK-ENDING

**PATH-B: VIOLENT-SUPPRESSION**
- Requirements: All-Aggressive-Choices
- Outcome: Riot-Police-Clear-Platz-by-Force
- Result: F-RANK-ENDING

**PATH-C: COMPROMISE**
- Requirements: Mixed-Choices
- Outcome: Partial-Agreement
- Result: A-or-B-RANK-ENDING

**PATH-D: CHAOS**
- Requirements: Inconsistent-Choices
- Outcome: Situation-Out-of-Control
- Result: C-RANK-ENDING

  - Tension-Final: Minus-Tension-Percent

- B-RANK: 60-74-Points (Good)

- F-RANK: 0-29-Points (Failure)

## ALL-SYSTEMS DELTA-SPECIFICATIONS

### CHARACTER-ANIMATION-DELTA-VALUES

**BLENDSHAPE-TRANSITION-DELTAS:**

**STANDARD-TRANSITION (Neutral-to-Full):**
- Duration: 0.3-Seconds (18-Frames-at-60fps)
- Delta-per-Frame: 1.0 / 18 = 0.0556 (5.56%-per-Frame)
- Delta-per-Second: 3.333
- Acceleration-Curve: ease-In-Out
  - Frames-1-6: Œî = 0.025 (slow-Start)
  - Frames-7-12: Œî = 0.0833 (fast-Middle)
  - Frames-13-18: Œî = 0.025 (slow-End)

**FAST-TRANSITION (Micro-Expression):**
- Duration: 0.1-Seconds (6-Frames)
- Delta-per-Frame: 1.0 / 6 = 0.1667 (16.67%-per-Frame)
- Delta-per-Second: 10.0
- Acceleration-Curve: linear

**SLOW-TRANSITION (Tired-Expression):**
- Duration: 1.0-Second (60-Frames)
- Delta-per-Frame: 1.0 / 60 = 0.0167 (1.67%-per-Frame)
- Delta-per-Second: 1.0
- Acceleration-Curve: ease-In

**BLENDSHAPE-COMBINATION-DELTAS:**

When-Multiple-Blendshapes-Active:
- Additive-Blending: Final = Œ£(Blendshape-Weight √ó Delta)
- Normalization-Threshold: if-Total > 1.0 ‚Üí normalize
- Normalization-Delta: reduce-All-by-Factor-per-Frame

Example-Frame-Calculation:
```
Frame-N:
  smile_L: 0.5 (Œî +0.05/frame)
  eyeSquint_L: 0.3 (Œî +0.03/frame)
  Total: 0.8

Frame-N+1:
  smile_L: 0.55
  eyeSquint_L: 0.33
  Total: 0.88

Frame-N+2:
  smile_L: 0.60
  eyeSquint_L: 0.36
  Total: 0.96
```

---

### PUPIL-DILATION-DELTA-VALUES

**LIGHTING-DRIVEN-DILATION:**

**BRIGHT-TO-DARK-TRANSITION:**
- Initial-Pupil-Size: 1.5mm (bright-Light)
- Final-Pupil-Size: 8.0mm (dark-Environment)
- Total-Delta: 6.5mm
- Duration: 0.5-Seconds (30-Frames)
- Delta-per-Frame: 6.5 / 30 = 0.217mm-per-Frame
- Delta-per-Second: 13.0mm-per-Second

**FRAME-BY-FRAME-BREAKDOWN:**
```
Frame-0: 1.50mm (bright)
Frame-1: 1.72mm (Œî +0.22)
Frame-2: 1.94mm (Œî +0.22)
Frame-3: 2.16mm (Œî +0.22)
...
Frame-15: 4.75mm (mid-Point, Œî accelerates)
...
Frame-29: 7.78mm (Œî +0.22)
Frame-30: 8.00mm (dark, final)
```

**ACCELERATION-CURVE (Biological-Realistic):**
- Frames-0-10: slow-Start (Œî = 0.15mm/frame)
- Frames-10-20: fast-Middle (Œî = 0.30mm/frame)
- Frames-20-30: slow-End (Œî = 0.15mm/frame)

**EMOTION-DRIVEN-DELTA:**

**FEAR-RESPONSE:**
- Trigger: Enemy-Appears
- Initial: 3.0mm (neutral)
- Peak: 7.0mm (dilated)
- Delta: 4.0mm
- Duration: 0.2-Seconds (12-Frames)
- Delta-per-Frame: 4.0 / 12 = 0.333mm-per-Frame
- Acceleration: instant-Jump (no-Ease)

**ANGER-RESPONSE:**
- Trigger: Provoked
- Initial: 3.0mm
- Constricted: 2.0mm
- Delta: -1.0mm
- Duration: 0.3-Seconds (18-Frames)
- Delta-per-Frame: -0.056mm-per-Frame

---

### EYE-MOVEMENT-DELTA-VALUES

**SACCADE-DELTA-SPECIFICATIONS:**

**FAST-SACCADE (Large-Distance):**
- Angular-Distance: 40-Degrees (max-Angle-from-Forward)
- Duration: 0.2-Seconds (12-Frames)
- Peak-Velocity: 900-Degrees-per-Second
- Delta-per-Frame: 40 / 12 = 3.33-Degrees-per-Frame (average)

**ACCELERATION-PROFILE:**
```
Frame-0: 0¬∞ (start)
Frame-1: Œî +2¬∞ (accelerate)
Frame-2: Œî +5¬∞ (peak-Speed)
Frame-3: Œî +8¬∞ (peak)
Frame-4: Œî +7¬∞ (peak)
Frame-5: Œî +6¬∞ (peak)
Frame-6: Œî +5¬∞ (peak)
Frame-7: Œî +3¬∞ (decelerate)

Frame-11: Œî -0.2¬∞ (correct-Back)

```
